<review>I started my journey at 377 lbs, all-time high BP of 230/110, and had high cholesterol and congestive heart failure. Then i hit rock bottom with cardiac arrest from atrial fibrillation. After having heart and weight loss surgery two years ago, I knew I needed to work physical activity into my lifestyle in order to continue forward on my journey.I knew OTF was the answer for me, because i had been a member a few years before, but my head just wasn't in the game at the time. Getting going wasn't easy. All the physical and mental sluggishness was there, but the coaches and staff are encouraging and welcoming. Most importantly, the other members are more of a community than a room full of random strangers. You form relationships. That's huge for keeping you motivated and accountable.The classes are well designed for complete and overall effectiveness, and to make sure you get the most out of your time, every time. Coaches demonstrate all the exercises, and offer alternatives and modifications to help with different fitness levels or physical limitations. My wife and I have found an overall fitness home at OTF, and going together is a part of our ongoing journey. Now, over 150 pounds lighter, regular BP, no cholesterol meds - no daily meds at all - I'm ready for that next Dri-Tri. But you'll see me at OT almost every day until then. Fitness is no longer a goal for me, it's a reality. OTF makes it easy, and rewarding, to stay on track.< /review><Resp>None<//Resp><rate>5<//rate><userid>100789425921164450510<//userid><name>Justin Prahar<//name>< Time>

I love OTF Roseville! The workouts are never the same and are always challenging.  The coaches are energetic and knowledgeable.  Once they get to know you, they find ways to challenge you on the cardio floor and weight floor -- they truly want to help you meet your goals.  They encourage you when you are wanting to slack off and are supportive when you are having an off day (or nursing an injury.)  The sales associates are friendly and greet everyone by name (I still haven't figured out how they know the names of 700 members--impressive!) I can't imagine my life without my daily dose of my OTF family.</Review>

<gmap_id>0x80dd29179979f929:0x75d111926a12abe3< /gmap_id><name>Nevaeh Nunez<//name>< time>
1614882664733<//time>
<userid>115183235729479992354<//userid>< response>
None<//response>
<text>This is a hidden gem.
Came here on a Saturday at around 8pm and there were many tables open.

Heads up: 2 order minimum for the grill. Also comes with your choice of soybean paste soup, kimchi soup or bean paste in hot pot for ($4.99 extra). We got the soybean paste soup and it's definitely one of the tastiest dwenjangjiggaes I've ever had. The server told us it is made ready to order (not pre cooked) and that it tastes almost like the Korean countryside. He was right! They also had a variety of banchans ranging from kimchi, picked jalape√±o, cucumber kimchi, pickled radish, a pickled onion salad, soybean sprouts and more.

Marinated short rib (28.99): the quality of the meat is 5 stars but I would say the marinade is 4 stars. I've definitely had better galbi marinades at other places. It was not as sweet and flavorful as I usually like. However, the amazing meat quality more than made up for it.

Rib finger (25.99): This was the star of the show. I normally don't like non-marinated meats when I go to kbbq places because the quality is not very good. However, the finger rib here was hands down one of the most tender, juicy and flavorful meats I've ever had. The quality of this meat was AMAZING. You must order this if you go.

The service was also amazing. Our server was very attentive, changed our grill multiple times, checked up on us often, made recommendations.

We will definitely be back! This place is comparable to the high quality ayce bbqs in Koreatown, LA but at a fraction of the price and wait.<//text><pictures>[{'url': <rating>3</rating>< Text>
A couple of things you need to know if you want to visit here: First, the menu is in Korean, and is not available in English. Communication with the servers is difficult if you do not speak Korean. The picture on the menu is a bit misleading. It shows a large plate full of meat next to the price of an individual entree, but is probably a picture of three or four entrees. Second, this place is a bit pricey for a hole in the wall strip mall in Stanton. The entrees for Korean BBQ were about $26 per person. The food was good, but not anything that I found super impressive.<//Text>

< name>
Grant Kindsfather< /name>
<Time>1564348356360< /Time><rating>5</rating>< Review>
In short, Burke & Redford Orthodontists changed my life. The staff are professionals, the offices are clean and I can't recommend them enough. In my adolescence, I went to countless consultations with various orthodontists, all of which considered my case severe, many of which recommended either surgery, tooth extractions, or both. Dr. Burke was the exception, his recommended approach was the least invasive and I couldn't be happier with the results.

I wore braces for four years throughout highschool, enduring both a palatal expander and a device known as a herbst appliance, it was a challenge but worth the payoff. At nearly every visit Dr. Burke was excited to see my results, you can really tell he is passionate about his work. Although it has been over a decade since I started my teeth straightening journey, there are many moments I still have immense gratitude.

Thank you Dr. Burke, Zabrina, Liz and everyone else at Burke & Redford Orthodontists, you've changed my life for the better.
(As a side note, my orthodontic treatment was done before Burke and Redford started their partnership, but the high quality of their work remains the same.)</Review>

< Review>
Dr. Burke was my orthodontist for 3 years. While I was in treatment, the staff was so friendly and helpful. Aileen, Liz and Johanna always made each visit (which could be scary with my fear of the dentist chair) very welcoming and comfortable. The receptionist, Zabrina, always made sure my appointments were scheduled and made each visit something to look forward to. She even remembered what was going on in my life and asked me about my family (knowing their names even!) each visit. The office, waiting area and restroom was always very clean and very organized. Dixie handled my payments, which were priced very fairly. And last but definitely not least, Dr. Burke was always so wonderful. You can definitely tell his main concern is making your smile beautiful the right way! He is always in such a wonderful mood and always seems so excited to see you! Whether it's his whistling while he works or cheery disposition, Dr. Burke is doing something right. The office even raffles off prizes (it was a new iPod when I was there) for great brushing! They also have an Xbox gaming system to keep your kiddos occupied and a fish tank that adds so much more life (if that's possible) to the office. My braces were removed 7 years ago and, with the help of this amazing staff, my teeth are still straight! I highly suggest going to Dr. Burke's office to get that beautiful smile you've always wanted as well as an awesome experience!</Review>
